function getCookieVal(offset) {
  var endstr = document.cookie.indexOf (";", offset);
  if(endstr == -1) endstr = document.cookie.length;
  return unescape(document.cookie.substring(offset, endstr));
}
function GetCookie(name) {
  var arg = name + "=";
  var alen = arg.length;
  var clen = document.cookie.length;
  var i = 0;
  while(i < clen) {
    var j = i + alen;
    if (document.cookie.substring(i, j) == arg) return getCookieVal (j);
    i = document.cookie.indexOf(" ", i) + 1;
    if (i == 0) break;
  }
  return "";
}
function getUserType() {
  return 1;
}

function sort(wordarray){
var tmp;
for (var i=0;i<9;i++){
        for (var j=0;j<9-i;j++){
                if (wordarray[j].length>wordarray[j+1].length) {
                        tmp = wordarray[j];
                        wordarray[j]=wordarray[j+1];
                        wordarray[j+1]=tmp;
                }
        }
}
}

      hotwordbox.style.left = (position[0] - 2) + "px";

function stopPropagation(e){

    }
}

var nextIdx = 0;
function getNextYdDefault() {var len = ydDefaults.length;if (nextIdx >= len) { nextIdx = 0;} var res = ydDefaults[nextIdx];nextIdx++; return res; }

function ydInputFocus(e,pos){
    if (oldui) {
	if(isYdDefault(e.value)) {
		e.className="yd-query";e.value='';
		clearHotIcon();
		return true;
	} 
    } else {
	if (e.className=='yd-defaultquery') {
		e.className="yd-query";e.value='';
		noUserInput=false;
	}
    }
	return false;
}

function getSearchUrl(inputId, product, keyfrom) {
   var url = "http://" + product + ".youdao.com/";
   if (window.RegExp && window.encodeURIComponent) {
     var input = document.getElementById(inputId);
     var query = input.value;
     if (isYdDefault(query)) query="";
     if (query != "") {
       query = query.replace(/(^link:)|(^inlink:)|(^related:)/,"");
       url = url+"search?q="+encodeURIComponent(query)+"&keyfrom="+keyfrom;
     } else {
       url = url+"?keyfrom="+keyfrom;
     }
   }
   return url;
}
function changeProduct(p) {
   var url = getSearchUrl("query", p, "163.index");
   window.open(url, "_blank");
   return false;
}
function clickYdSubmit() {
   var input = document.getElementById("query");
   var query = input.value;
   if (!isYdDefault(query)) {
     document.getElementById("ydForm").submit();
   } else {
	if (oldui){
	     changeHotWord("http://www.youdao.com/search?q="+query+"&keyfrom=163.index.indexhot");
	} else {
	     changeHotWord("http://www.youdao.com/search?q="+query+"&keyfrom=163.newindex");
	}
   }
   return false;
}

    	<div class="titleBar ui_tit38">
        	<h2 class="tit"><a href="http://2010.163.com/">亚运</a>·<a href="http://2010.163.com/">广州</a></h2>
            <span class="more"><a href="http://2010.163.com/photo/">图片</a> | <a href="http://2010.163.com/charity/">公益明星</a></span>
        </div>
        <div class="content">
        	<ul class="imgTxt90">
   <li class="clearfix">
               <a href="http://2010.163.com/jiayou/" title="美女主播为亚运加油"><img src="http://img5.cache.netease.com/gz2010/2010/4/16/20100416083712fa9e8.jpg" width="90" height="90" alt="美女主播为亚运加油" /></a>
               <h3 class="fB"><a href="http://2010.163.com/jiayou/" title="美女主播为亚运加油">美女主播为亚运加油</a></h3>
               <p class="f12px cGray">一起来，为亚运加油！美在花城冠军教你做亚运手势操。<span class="cDRed"><a href="http://2010.163.com/jiayou/">[详细]</a></span></p>
              </li>

(function() {
var china = {
	north : "|北京市|天津市|河北省|山西省|内蒙古|辽宁省|吉林省|黑龙江省|山东省|",

var locQuery = {
	url : "http://ip.ws.126.net/ipquery",
	cookieName : "locOfCh",
	exec : function(onComplete) {
		var result = NTES.cookie.get(this.cookieName);
		if (result != "" && china.hasOwnProperty(result)) {
			onComplete(result);
		} else {
			NTES.ajax.importJs(this.url, function() {
				if (typeof lo != "undefined" && typeof lc != "undefined") {
					var tempO = "|" + lo + "|", tempC = "|" + lc + "|";
					if (china.north.indexOf(tempO) != -1) {
						result = "north";
					} else if (china.east.indexOf(tempO) != -1) {
						result = "east";
					} else if (china.shenzhen.indexOf(tempC) != -1) {
						result = "shenzhen";
					} else {
						result = "others";
					}
				}
				if (result) {
					NTES.cookie.set(locQuery.cookieName, result, '1M',".163.com");
					onComplete(result);
				}
			});
		}
	}
};
houseIPQuery = locQuery;

(function(){
   var Util = {
       getXY: function (Obj) {
           var sumTop = 0, sumLeft = 0;
           while (Obj != document.body && Obj != null) {
               sumLeft += Obj.offsetLeft;
               sumTop += Obj.offsetTop;
               Obj = Obj.offsetParent;
           }
           return {
               x: sumLeft,
               y: sumTop
           };
       }
   };
   var SelectList = {
       username: false,
       usernameX: false,
       usernameY: false,
       usernameH: false,
       usernameList: false,
       curSelcetIndex: -1,
       selectdiv: "<div id =\"selectlist\"><table width=\"100%\" cellspacing=\"0\" cellpadding=\"0\" class=\"tableMain\"><tbody><tr><td><td /></tr></tbody></table><iframe style=\"display:block\" frameborder=\"0\" id=\"postiframe\" name=\"postiframe\"></iframe></div>",
       selectElement: false,
       domainArray: ["163.com", "126.com", "yeah.net", "188.com", "vip.163.com"],
       resizeFunc: function () {
           var ds = document.getElementById("selectlist");
           var username_x = Util.getXY(SelectList.username).x - 3;
           var username_y = Util.getXY(SelectList.username).y;
           ds.style.left = username_x + "px";
           ds.style.top = (username_y + SelectList.username.offsetHeight) + "px";
       },
       bind: function (obj) {
           this.username = obj;
           var xy = Util.getXY(this.username);
           this.usernameX = xy.x;
           this.emailY = xy.y;
           this.handle();
       },
       handle: function () {
           document.write(this.selectdiv);
           this.selectElement = document.getElementById("selectlist");
           this.usernameList = this.selectElement.firstChild.firstChild.rows[0].firstChild;
           this.curSelcetIndex = 0;
           this.username.onblur = function () {
               SelectList.doSelect();
           };
           try {
               this.username.addEventListener("keypress", this.keypressProc, false);
               this.username.addEventListener("keyup", this.keyupProc, false);
           }
           catch(e) {
               try {
                   this.username.attachEvent("onkeydown", this.checkKeyDown);
                   this.username.attachEvent("onkeypress", this.keypressProc);
                   this.username.attachEvent("onkeyup", this.keyupProc);
               }
               catch(e) {}
           }
           this.resizeFunc();
           if (navigator.userAgent.indexOf("MSIE") > 0) {
               window.attachEvent("onresize", this.resizeFunc);
           } else {
               window.onresize = this.resizeFunc;
           }
       },
       preventEvent: function (event) {
           event.cancelBubble = true;
           event.returnValue = false;
           if (event.preventDefault) {
               event.preventDefault();
           }
           if (event.stopPropagation) {
               event.stopPropagation();
           }
       },
       checkKeyDown: function (event) {
           this.curSelcetIndex = 0;
           var keyCode = event.keyCode;
           if (keyCode == 38 || keyCode == 40) {
               SelectList.clearFocus();
               if (keyCode == 38) {
                   SelectList.upSelectIndex();
               } else {
                   SelectList.downSelectIndex();
               }
               SelectList.setFocus();
           }
       },
       keyupProc: function (event) {
           this.curSelcetIndex = 0;
           var keyCode = event.keyCode;
           SelectList.changeUsernameSelect();
           if (keyCode == 13) {
               SelectList.doSelect();
           }
           var isSafari;
           if ((isSafari = navigator.userAgent.indexOf("Safari")) > 0) {
               if (keyCode == 38 || keyCode == 40) {
                   SelectList.preventEvent(event);
                   SelectList.clearFocus();
                   if (keyCode == 38) {
                       SelectList.upSelectIndex();
                   } else {
                       SelectList.downSelectIndex();
                   }
                   SelectList.setFocus();
               }
           }
       },
       keypressProc: function (event) {
           this.curSelcetIndex = 0;
           var keyCode = event.keyCode;
           if (keyCode == 13) {
               SelectList.preventEvent(event);
           } else {
               if (keyCode == 38 || keyCode == 40) {
                   SelectList.preventEvent(event);
                   SelectList.clearFocus();
                   if (keyCode == 38) {
                       SelectList.upSelectIndex();
                   } else {
                       SelectList.downSelectIndex();
                   }
                   SelectList.setFocus();
               } else {
                   if (keyCode == 108 || keyCode == 110 || keyCode == 111 || keyCode == 115) {
                       setTimeout("SelectList.changeUsernameSelect()", 20);
                   }
               }
           }
       },
       clearFocus: function (index) {
           var index = this.curSelcetIndex;
           try {
               var x = this.findTdElement(index);
               x.style.backgroundColor = "white";
           }
           catch(e) {}
       },
       findTdElement: function (index) {
           try {
               var x = this.usernameList.firstChild.rows;
               for (var i = 0; i < x.length; ++i) {
                   if (x[i].firstChild.idx == index) {
                       return x[i].firstChild;
                   }
               }
           }
           catch(e) {}
           return false;
       },
       upSelectIndex: function () {
           var index = this.curSelcetIndex;
           if (this.usernameList.firstChild == null) {
               return;
           }
           var x = this.usernameList.firstChild.rows;
           var i;
           for (i = 0; i < x.length; ++i) {
               if (x[i].firstChild.idx == index) {
                   break;
               }
           }
           if (i == 0) {
               this.curSelcetIndex = (x.length - 1);
           } else {
               this.curSelcetIndex = x[i - 1].firstChild.idx;
           }
       },
       downSelectIndex: function () {
           var index = this.curSelcetIndex;
           if (this.usernameList.firstChild == null) {
               return;
           }
           var x = this.usernameList.firstChild.rows;
           var i = 0;
           for (; i < x.length; ++i) {
               if (x[i].firstChild.idx == index) {
                   break;
               }
           }
           if (i >= x.length - 1) {
               this.curSelcetIndex = x[0].firstChild.idx;
           } else {
               this.curSelcetIndex = x[i + 1].firstChild.idx;
           }
       },
       setFocus: function () {
           var index = this.curSelcetIndex;
           try {
               var x = this.findTdElement(index);
               x.style.backgroundColor = "#85B6EA";
               x.style.cursor = "pointer";
           }
           catch(e) {}
       },
       changeUsernameSelect: function () {
           var userInput = this.username.value;
           if (userInput.trim() == "") {
               this.selectElement.style.display = "none";
           } else {
               var username = "",
                   hostname = "";
               var pos;
               if ((pos = userInput.indexOf("@")) < 0) {
                   username = userInput;
                   hostname = "";
               } else {
                   username = userInput.substr(0, pos);
                   hostname = userInput.substr(pos + 1, userInput.length);
               }
               var usernames = [];
               if (hostname == "") {
                   for (var i = 0; i < this.domainArray.length; ++i) {
                       usernames.push(username + "@" + this.domainArray[i]);
                   }
               } else {
                   for (var i = 0; i < this.domainArray.length; ++i) {
                       //if (this.domainArray[i].indexOf(hostname) == 0) {
                           usernames.push(username + "@" + this.domainArray[i]);
                       //}
                   }
               }
               if (usernames.length > 0) {
                   this.resizeFunc();
                   this.selectElement.style.zIndex = "100";
                   this.selectElement.style.backgroundColor = "white";
                   this.selectElement.style.display = "block";
                   var myTable = document.createElement("TABLE");
                   myTable.cellSpacing = 0;
                   myTable.cellPadding = 3;
                   myTable.width = "100%";
                   var tbody = document.createElement("TBODY");
                   myTable.appendChild(tbody);
                   for (var i = 0; i < usernames.length; ++i) {
                       var tr = document.createElement("TR");
                       var td = document.createElement("TD");
                       td.nowrap = "true";
                       td.align = "left";
                       td.innerHTML = usernames[i];
                       td.idx = i;
                       td.onmouseover = function () {
                           SelectList.clearFocus();
                           SelectList.curSelcetIndex = this.idx;
                           SelectList.setFocus();
                           this.style.cursor = "pointer";
                       };
                       td.onmouseout = function () {};
                       td.onclick = function () {
                           SelectList.doSelect();
                       };
                       tr.appendChild(td);
                       tbody.appendChild(tr);
                   }
                   this.usernameList.innerHTML = "";
                   this.usernameList.appendChild(myTable);
                   this.setFocus();
               } else {
                   this.selectElement.style.display = "none";
                   this.curSelcetIndex = -1;
               }
           }
       },
       doSelect: function () {
           this.selectElement.style.display = "none";
           if (this.username.value.trim() == "") {
               return;
           }
           if( this.curSelcetIndex == -1 && this.username.value.trim().indexOf("@") == -1) {
               this.curSelcetIndex = 0;
           }
           var currentUsernameTd = this.findTdElement(this.curSelcetIndex);
           if (currentUsernameTd && !/^@.+$/.test(this.username.value.trim()) ) {
                this.username.value = currentUsernameTd.innerHTML;
           }
           userNameTips.hide();
           $("#password").focus();
           if( NTES.browser.msie ) {
              var r = $("#password").createTextRange(); 
              r.collapse(false);
              r.select();
           }
       }
   };
   var body = $(document.body), doc = $(document.documentElement);
   var P_INFO = NTES.cookie.get("P_INFO");

   var SELECT_VALUE = NTES.cookie.get("selectValue");
   var CLOSE_NUM = NTES.cookie.get("closeNum");

   NTES.ui.PopUpLayer = function (ctrl, content) {
        if (!arguments.length) {
            return;
        }
        var t = this;
        t.constructor = arguments.callee;
        t._clickElement = ctrl;
        t._contentElement = content;
        t._clearTimeout = null;
        t._timeout = 300;
        t._clickElement.addEvent("click", t.clickHandle.bind(t));
        t._clickElement.addEvent("mouseover", t.mouseOverHandle.bind(t));
        t._clickElement.addEvent("mouseout", t.mouseOutHandle.bind(t));
        t._contentElement.addEvent("mouseover", t.mouseOverHandle.bind(t));
        t._contentElement.addEvent("mouseout", t.mouseOutHandle.bind(t));
   };
   NTES.ui.PopUpLayer.prototype = {
        clickHandle: function(e) {
            e = e || window.event;
            if( e.stopPropagation ){
                e.stopPropagation();
            } else {
                e.cancelBubble = true;
            }
            var t = this;
            if( t._contentElement.style.display !== "block" ) {
                t._contentElement.style.display = "block";
                doc.addEvent("mousedown", documentEvent);
                t.changeSelectList();
            } else {
                t._contentElement.style.display = "none";
                doc.removeEvent("mousedown", documentEvent);
            }
        },
        changeSelectList : function(){
            var t = indexLoginObj;
            t.selectListBindEvent(t.getMailType());
            if( SELECT_VALUE && SELECT_VALUE == t._selectInput.value ) {
               t._selectAllList[t._selectInput.value].style.background = "#85B6EA";
               t._selectAllList[t._selectInput.value].style.color = "#fff";
            }
        },
        mouseOverHandle: function() {
            var t = this;
            t._clearTimeout && clearTimeout( t._clearTimeout );
        },
        mouseOutHandle: function() {
             var t = this;
             t._clearTimeout = window.setTimeout(function(){
                t._contentElement.style.display = "none";
             },t._timeout);
        }
   };

      init : function() {

      userNameFocusEvent : function(){
           var t = this;
           t._userNameTips.hide();
           t._oldUserNameValue = t._userName.value.trim();
      },
      passwordFocusEvent : function(){
           var t = this;
           t._passWordTips.hide();
      },
      getMailType : function(){
           var t = this, mailType = "";
           if( /@([^\.]+)/.test(t._userName.value) ){
              mailType = RegExp.$1;
              if( t._mailArray.indexOf(mailType) == -1 ) {
                  mailType = "others";
              }
           }
           return mailType;
      },
      userNameBlurEvent : function(){
           var t = this, mailType = t.getMailType();
           if (t._userName.value.trim() == "") {
               return;
           }
           if( mailType == "188" && t._selectInput.value != 4 ){
                t._select.innerHTML = "选择去向";
               t._selectInput.value = "4";
               return;
           }
           if( t._selectInput.value == 1 || t._selectInput.value == 2 || t._selectInput.value == 3 || t._selectInput.value == 4 || t._selectInput.value == 5 || ( mailType == "others" && t._selectInput.value == "" ) ) {
               if( t._mailArray[t._selectInput.value] !== mailType ) {
                   t._select.innerHTML = "选择去向";
                   t._selectInput.value = "";
               }
           }
           if( t._oldUserNameValue != t._userName.value.trim() ) {
               $("#password").value = "";
           }
       },
       selectListBindEvent : function( mailType ){
           var t = this;
           var xhtml = [], tempObj = {};
           for( var i = 0, len = t._selectTextArray.length; i < len; i++ ) {
               tempObj = { "disable" : t._mailSelectArray[mailType][i] }
               xhtml.push( NTES.util.parseTpl(t._selectTextArray[i], tempObj) );
           }
           xhtml.join("");
           t._selectMain.innerHTML = xhtml.toString().replace(/\,/g,"");
           t._selectAllList = $("li", t._selectMain);
           t._selectList = $("li[used!=disable]", t._selectMain);
           t._selectList.addEvent("click", function (e) {
                e = e || window.event;
                if( e.stopPropagation ) {
                    e.stopPropagation();
                } else {
                    e.cancelBubble = true;
                }
                t._selectInput.value = t._selectAllList.indexOf(this);
                t._select.innerHTML = this.innerHTML;
                if ( t._userName.value.trim() == "" ) {
                   t._userName.value = this.title;
                   if( t._userName.createTextRange ) {/*设置光标*/
                      var range = t._userName.createTextRange();
                      range.move("character", 0);
                      range.select();
                   } else {
                      t._userName.focus();
                      t._userName.setSelectionRange(0, 0);
                   }
                } else {
                   t._passWord.focus();
                }
                t._selectMain.style.display = "none";
           });
           t._selectList.addEvent("mouseover", function () {
               this.style.background = "#85B6EA";
               this.style.color = "#fff";
           });
           t._selectList.addEvent("mouseout", function () {
               this.style.background = "none";
               this.style.color = "#4b4b4b";
           });
       },
       checkInput : function(){
           var t = this;
           if( t._userName.value.trim() === "" ) {
               t._userName.focus();
               setTimeout(function(){
                  t._userNameTips.waring("请输入用户名");
               },0);               
               setTimeout(function(){
                  t._userNameTips.hide();
               }, 3000);
               return false;
           }
           if( t._passWord.value === "" ) {
               t._passWord.focus();
               t._passWordTips.waring("请输入密码");
               setTimeout(function(){
                  t._passWordTips.hide();
               }, 3000);
               return false;
           }
           return true;
       },
       loginSubmit : function(e){
           e.preventDefault();
           var t = this;
           if( typeof mobileTips != "undefined" && mobileTips._wrapper.parentNode ) {
               mobileTips._wrapper.parentNode.removeChild(mobileTips._wrapper);
           }
           if( t.checkInput() ) {
                t._loginForm.target = "_blank";
               if( t._select.innerHTML == "选择去向" || t.getMailType() == "others" ) {
                   NTES.cookie.set("selectValue", "", 30 * 24 * 60);
                   t._userName.name = "username";
                   t._passWord.name = "password";
                   if( t._select.innerHTML == "选择去向" ) {
                        t._loginForm.target = "_self";
                   }
                   t._loginForm.action = t._formRequestArray[0];
               } else {
                   NTES.cookie.set("selectValue", t._selectInput.value, 30 * 24 * 60);
                   switch (parseInt(t._selectInput.value)) {
                      case 0:
                          t._userName.name = "username";
                          t._passWord.name = "password";
                          t._loginForm.action = t._formRequestArray[t._selectInput.value];
                          break;
                      case 1:
                          t._userName.name = "username";
                          t._passWord.name = "password";
                          t._loginForm.action = t._formRequestArray[t._selectInput.value];
                          break;
                      case 4:
                          t._userName.name = "user";
                          t._passWord.name = "pass";
                          t._loginForm.action = t._formRequestArray[t._selectInput.value];
                          break;
                      default:
                          t._userName.name = "user";
                          t._passWord.name = "password";
                          t._ursName.name = "username";
                          t._ursName.value = t._userName.value;
                          t._loginForm.action = t._formRequestArray[t._selectInput.value];
                          break;
                   }
               }
               t._loginForm.submit();
           }
       },
       closeMobile : function() {
           var t = this;
           mobileTips._wrapper.parentNode.removeChild(mobileTips._wrapper);
       	   NTES.cookie.set("closeNum", CLOSE_NUM+1 , 30 * 24 * 60);
       }
   };
   function documentEvent(e) {
       var thisObj = e.target ? e.target : event.srcElement;
       do {
           if (thisObj.id == "select_main" || thisObj.id == "selected") return;
           if (thisObj.tagName.toUpperCase() == 'BODY' || thisObj.tagName.toUpperCase() == 'HTML') {
               $("#select_main").style.display = "none";
               doc.removeEvent("mousedown", documentEvent);
               return;
           };
           thisObj = thisObj.parentNode;
       } while (thisObj.parentNode);
   };
   NTES.ui.Tips = function( node, flag, _switch ){
       if (!arguments.length) {
           return;
       }
       var t = this;
       t.constructor = arguments.callee;
       t._node = node;
       t._flag = flag;
       t._timerId = null;
       var elem = document.createElement("div");
       elem.style.float = "left";
       elem.style.background = "#FFFCF0";
       elem.style.border = "1px solid #dcdddd";
       elem.style.padding = "2px";
       elem.style.display = "none";
       elem.style.position = "absolute";
       body.appendChild(elem);
       t._wrapper = elem;
       if( t._flag ){
          t._node.addEvent("mouseover", function(){
             if( typeof mobileTips != "undefined" && ( t._node.value.trim() != "" ) && ( mobileTips._wrapper.style.display != "none" ) ) {
                 mobileTips._wrapper.style.display = "none";
             }
             t.show.call(t);
          });
       }
       if( _switch ) {
         t._node.addEvent("mouseout", function(){
             if( t._flag ) {
                if( typeof mobileTips != "undefined" && ( mobileTips._wrapper.style.display != "block" ) ) {
                    mobileTips._wrapper.style.display = "block";
                }
             }
             t.hide.call(t);
         });;
       }
   };
   NTES.ui.Tips.prototype = {
       show : function( title ) {
          var t = this;
          
          var position = t.fetchOffset();
          t._wrapper.style.top = ( position.top + t._node.offsetHeight )+"px";
          t._wrapper.style.left = ( position.left - 4 )+"px";
          if( title ) {
             t._wrapper.innerHTML = title;
             t._wrapper.style.display = "block";
          } else if( t._node.value.trim() != "" ){
             t._wrapper.innerHTML = t._node.value.trim();
             t._wrapper.style.display = "block";
          }
       },
       hide : function() {
          var t = this;
          t._wrapper.style.display = "none";
       },
       waring : function( title ){
           var t = this;
           t.show( title );
       },
       fetchOffset: function(){
           var t = this;
           var obj = t._node, left_offset = obj.offsetLeft , top_offset = obj.offsetTop;
           while ((obj = obj.offsetParent) != null) {
               left_offset += obj.offsetLeft;
               top_offset += obj.offsetTop;
           }
           return { 'left' : left_offset, 'top' : top_offset };
       }
  };

  indexLoginObj.init();
})();
(function () {    
    NTES.ui.DelaySlide = function (ctrls, contents, css, delay) {
        if (!arguments.length) {
            return;
        }
        var t = this;
        t.total = contents.length;
        if (ctrls && t.total !== ctrls.length) {
            throw "can not match ctrls(" + ctrls.length + ") and contents(" + t.total + ")";
        }
        t.constructor = arguments.callee;
        t._curIndex = -1;
        t._ctrls = ctrls;
        t._contents = contents;
        t._css = css;
        t._delay = delay;
        if (t._ctrls && t._ctrls.length) {
            var change = function (e, index) {
                this._delayTimer = setTimeout(this.show.bind(this, index), this._delay);
                e.preventDefault();
            }.bind(t),
                preventChange = function () {
                this._delayTimer && clearTimeout(this._delayTimer);
            }.bind(t);
            for (var i = t.total - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
                NTES.event.addEvent(t._ctrls[i], "mouseover", change, new Number(i));
                NTES.event.addEvent(t._ctrls[i], "mouseout", preventChange);
            }
        }
    };
    NTES.ui.DelaySlide.prototype = {
        show: function (index) {
            var t = this;
            index = index < 0 ? 0 : index >= t.total ? t.total - 1 : index;
            var ctrl = t._ctrls ? t._ctrls[index] : null,
            content = t._contents[index];
            if (-1 === t._curIndex) {
                t._curIndex = 0;
            }
            NTES.style.removeCss(t._ctrls, t._css);
            NTES.style.removeCss(t._contents, t._css);
            NTES.style.addCss(ctrl, t._css);
            NTES.style.addCss(content, t._css);
            t.onShow && t.onShow(index, ctrl, content);
            t._curIndex = index;
        }
    };
    var slides = ["news", "vedio", "ent", "sports", "money", "house", "lady", "tech", "auto","luntan", "blog", "cRn1"],
        i, wrapper;
    for (i = slides.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
        wrapper = $("#" + slides[i]);
        new NTES.ui.DelaySlide(wrapper.$("span.con"), wrapper.$("div.content"), "current", 150);
    }
    var slides = ["cAn1_l", "cAn1_r"],
        i, wrapper;
    for (i = slides.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
        wrapper = $("#" + slides[i]);
        wrapper && (new NTES.ui.DelaySlide(wrapper.$("li"), wrapper.$("div.normal"), "current", 150));
    }
})();

    lastAdText = parseInt(NTES.cookie.get("NTES_adText")),
    curAdText;
if (isNaN(lastAdText)) {
    curAdText = 0;
} else {
    curAdText = lastAdText + 1;
    if (curAdText >= NTES("#cRn1 span.con").length) {
        curAdText = 0;
    }
    ad_Text.show(curAdText);
}
NTES.cookie.set("NTES_adText", curAdText, 30 * 24 * 60);
// 股票搜索导航框
var stockSuggest = new ntesStockSuggest({
	// 输入框id
	inputid: "stockCode",
	// 记录数
	max: 10,
	tooltip: "输入代码",
	// 左对齐的元素, 没有则按输入框
	posElem: "stockCode",
	// 获取查询类型HS/HK/US/...
	getType: function(){
		return "";
	},
	// 选中某一项
	callback: function(item){
		typeMap = {
			"SH":"http://quotes.money.163.com/0{0}.html",
			"SZ":"http://quotes.money.163.com/1{0}.html",
			"HK":"http://hkquotes.money.163.com/html/{0}.html",
			"FX":"http://quotes.money.163.com/forex/hq/{0}.html",
			"US":"http://quotes.money.163.com/usstock/hq/{0}.html",
			"FN":"http://quotes.fund.163.com/html/{0}.html",
			"FU":"http://quotes.money.163.com/futures/hq/{0}.html"
		};
		url = typeMap[item["type"]].replace("{0}",  item["symbol"]);
		window.open(url);
	}
});
// 点击查行情
function btnstocksearch(){
	if(stockSuggest.aSug.length==1){
		stockSuggest.oP.callback(stockSuggest.aSug[0]);
	}else{
		alert("请选择要查看的股票");
	}
}
function openwindow(url) {
window.open(url, "newwindow", "width=965,height=595,status=1,resizable=1,scrollbars=0,toolbar=0,menubar=0,titlebar=0,directories=0");
}
(function() {
var re_videoLink = /^(?:http:\/\/v.163.com\/column\/)|(?:http:\/\/v.163.com\/video\/)/i, links = $("a"), i = -1, len = links.length;
function setOpenWindow(e) {
	e.preventDefault();
	openwindow(this.href);
}
while (++i < len) {
	re_videoLink.test(links[i].href) && NTES.event.addEvent(links[i], "click", setOpenWindow);
}
})();

function weather4Youdao(city) {
  var url = "http://img3.126.net/yodaoimages/new_weather/201004151801/" + getCityId(city);
  var scriptDiv=document.getElementById("ydWeatherScript");
  while(scriptDiv.childNodes.length>0){
    scriptDiv.removeChild(scriptDiv.firstChild);
  }
  var script = document.createElement('script');
  script.src = url;
  script.charset = "gbk";
  scriptDiv.appendChild(script);
}

  }else{
    weatherAddr="北京";
  }
  NTES.cookie.set("ydWeatherAddr", weatherAddr, 365*24*60, "www.163.com");
}
if(weatherAddr.indexOf(" ") > 0) {
  var addr=weatherAddr.split(" ");
  weatherAddr=addr[0];
}
if(weatherAddr.charAt(weatherAddr.length-1) == '市') {
  weatherAddr = weatherAddr.substring(0, weatherAddr.length-1);
} 
weather4Youdao(weatherAddr);
